If you move, go to www.uscis.gov/addresschange to give us your new mailing address.

The notice explains why we transferred your case. Please follow the instructions in the notice. If you do not receive your notice by October 26, 2022, please go to www.uscis.gov/e-request to request a copy of the notice. If you move, go to www.uscis.gov/addresschange to give us your new mailing address.
